Grok 4.1 Fast (orange dot) tops at ~100% score for ~$105 cost, outperforming GPT-5 high (~80%/$150+), Gemini 3 Pro (~70%/$120), Claude 4.5 Sonnet (~60%/$130), and Grok 4 Fast (~50%/$100). Verified by independent evaluator Artificial Analysis.
